    policy-statement ARBOR-CLEAN-export-vrf {
        term ARBOR-CLEAN_TARGET_EXPORT {
            from protocol bgp;
            then {
                community add ARBOR-CLEAN-ROUTE-TARGET;
                accept;
            }
        }
        term REJECT-ALL {
            then reject;
        }
    }
    policy-statement ARBOR-CLEAN-import-vrf {
        term ARBOR-CLEAN_TARGET_IMPORT {
            from {
                protocol bgp;
                community ARBOR-CLEAN-ROUTE-TARGET;
            }
            then accept;
        }
        term REJECT-ALL {
            then reject;
        }
    }
    policy-statement ARBOR-NHS {
        term 1 {
            from {
                protocol bgp;
                route-type internal;
            }
            then {
                next-hop self;
            }
        }
    }
    policy-statement ARBOR-TMS {
        term WHOLESALE {
            from {
                community ARBOR-WHOLE-SALE;
                route-filter 0.0.0.0/0 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
            }
            then {
                community set ARBOR-RY-TMS;
                community add no-export;
                accept;
            }
        }
        term accept-all {
            from {
                route-filter 0.0.0.0/0 prefix-length-range /32-/32;
            }
            then {
                community set no-advertise;
                accept;
            }
        }
        term reject-all {
            then reject;
        }
    }

        }

                drop-probability [ 0 100 ];
            }
        }
    }
    forwarding-classes {
        class NC queue-num 3 priority high;
        class VOICE queue-num 5 priority high;
        class VIDEO queue-num 4 priority high;
        class BUSINESS queue-num 2 priority high;
        class PREMIUM-DATA queue-num 1 priority low;
        class BEST-EFFORT queue-num 0 priority low;
    }
    rewrite-rules {
        dscp DSCP_CORE_RW {
            forwarding-class NC {
                loss-priority low code-point cs6;
            }
            forwarding-class VOICE {
                loss-priority low code-point ef;
            }
            forwarding-class VIDEO {
                loss-priority low code-point af42;
            }
            forwarding-class BUSINESS {
                loss-priority low code-point af31;
                loss-priority high code-point af32;

            forwarding-class PREMIUM-DATA {

            }

                loss-priority low code-point be;
                loss-priority high code-point be;
            }
        }
        dscp DSCP_IPSLA_IGW_RW {

            }

            }
        }

            }

            forwarding-class NC {
                loss-priority low code-point 011;
            }

            }
            forwarding-class VIDEO {

            }
            forwarding-class BUSINESS {

                loss-priority high code-point 001;
            }
            forwarding-class PREMIUM-DATA {

                loss-priority high code-point 100;
            }
            forwarding-class BEST-EFFORT {
                loss-priority low code-point 000;
                loss-priority high code-point 000;
            }
        }

    scheduler-maps {

        }

        }

    schedulers {
        680M {
            transmit-rate {
                900m;
                exact;
            }
        }
        680M-Q {
            transmit-rate {
                900m;
                rate-limit;
            }
        }
        NC_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 1;
            buffer-size percent 1;
            priority high;
        }
        VOICE_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 10;
            buffer-size temporal 10k;
            priority high;
        }
        VEDIO_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 15;
            buffer-size percent 15;
            priority medium-high;
        }
        BUSINESS_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 10;
            buffer-size percent 10;
            priority medium-low;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority low protocol any drop-profile DP_SOFT;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority high protocol any drop-profile DP_MOD;
        }
        PREMIUM-DATA_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 15;
            buffer-size percent 15;
            priority low;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority low protocol any drop-profile DP_MOD;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority high protocol any drop-profile DP_AGGR;
        }
        BEST-EFFORT_SCH {
            transmit-rate {
                remainder;
            }
            buffer-size {
                remainder;
            }
            priority low;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority low protocol any drop-profile DP_MOD;
            drop-profile-map loss-priority high protocol any drop-profile DP_AGGR;
        }
        VIDEO_SCH {
            transmit-rate percent 15;
            buffer-size percent 15;
            priority medium-high;
        }
    }

        filter PROTECT-RE {
            term fragment-first {
                from {
                    first-fragment;
                }
                then {
                    count DDOS-FRAGMENT;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term fragment-is {
                from {
                    is-fragment;
                }
                then {
                    count DDOS-FRAGMENT;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term SMALL-PACKETS {
                from {
                    packet-length 0-24;
                }
                then {
                    count SMALL-PACKET-ATTACK;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term TCP-DOS-PROTECTION {
                from {
                    /* all incoming TCP based sessions i.e. only SYN */
                    source-prefix-list {
                        BGP-ADDRESSES;
                        LOCALHOST;
                        MGMT-ADDRESSES;
                    }
                    protocol tcp;
                    tcp-flags "(syn & !ack) | fin | rst";
                }
                then {
                    policer TCP-CONNECTION-POLICER;
                    count TCP-SYN;
                    next term;
                }
            }

            term ICMPV6_TRUSTED {

                    }

                    next-header icmpv6;
                    hop-limit 255;
                }
                then accept;

                from {
                    next-header icmpv6;
                    icmp-type [ echo-request echo-reply time-exceeded destination-unreachable packet-too-big parameter-problem ];

                }
            }

                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        WIREFILTER-8006-PROXY-4-v6;
                    }
                    next-header tcp;
                    destination-port [ http https 81 85 3128 8000 8080 8088 8089 8888 8443 591 8008 8081 8090 ];
                }
                then {
                    routing-instance WIREFILTER-8006-4-PROXY; ## 'WIREFILTER-8006-4-PROXY' is not defined
                }
            }
            term REDIRECT-TO-WIREFILTER-8006-5-v6 {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        WIREFILTER-8006-PROXY-5-v6;
                    }
                    next-header tcp;
                    destination-port [ http https 81 85 3128 8000 8080 8088 8089 8888 8443 591 8008 8081 8090 ];
                }
                then {
                    routing-instance WIREFILTER-8006-5-PROXY; ## 'WIREFILTER-8006-5-PROXY' is not defined
                }
            }
            term REDIRECT-TO-WIREFILTER-8006-6-v6 {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        WIREFILTER-8006-PROXY-6-v6;
                    }
                    next-header tcp;
                    destination-port [ http https 81 85 3128 8000 8080 8088 8089 8888 591 8008 8081 8090 ];
                }
                then {
                    routing-instance WIREFILTER-8006-6-PROXY; ## 'WIREFILTER-8006-6-PROXY' is not defined
                }
            }
            term REDIRECT-TO-WIREFILTER-8006 {
                from {
                    source-prefix-list {
                        TO-WIREFILTER-v6;
                        Sahara-ipv6-prefixes;
                    }
                    next-header tcp;
                    destination-port [ http https 81 85 3128 8000 8080 8088 8089 8888 8443 591 8008 8081 8090 ];
                }
                then {
                    routing-instance WIREFILTER-8006; ## 'WIREFILTER-8006' is not defined
                }
            }
            term REDIRECT-UNKNOWN-v6 {
                from {
                    next-header tcp;
                    destination-port [ http https 81 85 3128 8000 8080 8088 8089 8888 8443 591 8008 8081 8090 ];
                }
                then {
                    count REDIRECT-UNKNOWN-IPv6;
                    discard;
                }
            }
            term EXPLICIT-DEFAULT-v6 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
        filter ACCEPT-ALL-IPv6-IN {
            term 1 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
        filter ACCEPT-ALL-IPv6-OUT {
            term 1 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
    }
    family mpls {
        filter cos-test {
            term 1 {
                from {
                    exp [ 3 2 ];
                }
                then {
                    count exp-011;
                    accept;
                }
            }
            term 2 {
                then accept;
            }
        }
    }
    family bridge {
        filter WF-BW-LIMIT {
            term 1 {
                then {
                    policer WIREFIlTER;
                    accept;
                }
            }
        }
    }
    policer NTP-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 500k;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer SMALL-BW-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 1m;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer SNMP-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 2m;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer SSH-TELNET-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 25m;
            burst-size-limit 128k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer TCP-CONNECTION-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            /* approx 100 connections per second */
            bandwidth-limit 50k;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer VRRP-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 1m;
            burst-size-limit 128k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer ICMP-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 100m;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer ISP-LINK-PING-POLICER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 15m;
            burst-size-limit 15k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer WIREFIlTER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 680m;
            burst-size-limit 512k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer test-WIREFIlTER {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 400m;
            burst-size-limit 512k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer STM-4 {
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 622m;
            burst-size-limit 512k;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    policer Policer-UDP250Mbps {
        filter-specific;
        if-exceeding {
            bandwidth-limit 250m;
            burst-size-limit 12m;
        }
        then discard;
    }
    filter ficmp {
        term ticmp {
            from {
                source-address {
                    10.11.15.5/32;
                }
                packet-length 1400-1600;
            }
            then count cicmp;
        }
    }
}
